<s> The next question reveals what Beaupere had been leading up to: "Was it a feast-day" </s>
<s> You see </s>
<s> The suggestion that a voice coming from God would hardly advise or permit the violation, by war and bloodshed, of a sacred day </s>

<s> "Now, then, tell the this: did you hold it right to make the attack on such a day" </s>

<s> There was immediate silence in the court and intense expectancy noticeable all about </s>

<s> The trap had been long and laboriously prepared; it fell, and was empty </s>
<s> The court rose </s>
<s> It had sat for hours, and was cruelly fatigued </s>
<s> Most of the time had been taken up with apparently idle and purposeless inquiries about the Chinon events, the exiled Duke of Orleans, Joan's first proclamation, and so on, but all this seemingly random stuff had really been sown thick with hidden traps </s>
<s> But Joan had fortunately escaped them all, some by the protecting luck which attends upon ignorance and innocence, some by happy accident, the others by force of her best and surest helper, the clear vision and lightning intuitions of her extraordinary mind </s>
<s> Now, then, this daily baiting and badgering of this friendless girl, a captive in chains, was to continue a long, long time--dignified sport, a kennel of mastiffs and bloodhounds harassing a kitten!--and I may as well tell you, upon sworn testimony, what it was like from the first day to the last </s>
<s> When poor Joan had been in her grave a quarter of a century, the Pope called together that great court which was to re-examine her history, and whose just verdict cleared her illustrious name from every spot and stain, and laid upon the verdict and conduct of our Rouen tribunal the blight of its everlasting execrations </s>
<s> Manchon and several of the judges who had been members of our court were among the witnesses who appeared before that Tribunal of Rehabilitation </s>
<s> Recalling these miserable proceedings which I have been telling you about, Manchon testified thus:--here you have it, all in fair print in the unofficial history: When Joan spoke of her apparitions she was interrupted at almost every word </s>
<s> They wearied her with long and multiplied interrogatories upon all sorts of things </s>
<s> Almost every day the interrogatories of the morning lasted three or four hours; then from these morning interrogatories they extracted the particularly difficult and subtle points, and these served as material for the afternoon interrogatories, which lasted two or three hours </s>
<s> Moment by moment they skipped from one subject to another; yet in spite of this she always responded with an astonishing wisdom and memory </s>
<s> She often corrected the judges, saying, "But I have already answered that once before--ask the recorder," referring them to me </s>
<s> And here is the testimony of one of Joan's judges </s>
<s> Remember, these witnesses are not talking about two or three days, they are talking about a tedious long procession of days: They asked her profound questions, but she extricated herself quite well </s>
<s> Sometimes the questioners changed suddenly and passed on to another subject to see if she would not contradict herself </s>
<s> They burdened her with long interrogatories of two or three hours, from which the judges themselves went forth fatigued </s>
<s> From the snares with which she was beset the expertest man in the world could not have extricated himself but with difficulty </s>
<s> She gave her responses with great prudence; indeed to such a degree that during three weeks I believed she was inspired </s>
<s> Ah, had she a mind such as I have described </s>
<s> You see what these priests say under oath--picked men, men chosen for their places in that terrible court on account of their learning, their experience, their keen and practised intellects, and their strong bias against the prisoner </s>
<s> They make that poor country-girl out the match, and more than the match, of the sixty-two trained adepts </s>
<s> Isn't it so </s>
<s> They from the University of Paris, she from the sheepfold and the cow-stable </s>
<s> Ah, yes, she was great, she was wonderful </s>
<s> It took six thousand years to produce her; her like will not be seen in the earth again in fifty thousand </s>
<s> Such is my opinion </s>
<s> 7 Craft That Was in Vain THE THIRD meeting of the court was in that same spacious chamber, next day, 24th of February </s>
<s> How did it begin </s>
<s> In just the same old way </s>
<s> When the preparations were ended, the robed sixty-two massed in their chairs and the guards and order-keepers distributed to their stations, Cauchon spoke from his throne and commanded Joan to lay her hands upon the Gospels and swear to tell the truth concerning everything asked her </s>
<s> Joan's eyes kindled, and she rose; rose and stood, fine and noble, and faced toward the Bishop and said: "Take care what you do, my lord, you who are my judge, for you take a terrible responsibility on yourself and you presume too far" </s>
<s> It made a great stir, and Cauchon burst out upon her with an awful threat--the threat of instant condemnation unless she obeyed </s>

<s> This made a great tumult, and part of it was applause from the spectators </s>
<s> Joan resumed her seat </s>
<s> The Bishop still insisted </s>
<s> Joan said: "I have already made oath </s>

<s> I have sworn already </s>
<s> It is enough" </s>

<s> Why, religion was her life </s>

<s> It never contradicts itself </s>

<s> The court saw the priest's game, and watched his play with a cruel eagerness </s>
<s> Poor Joan was grown dreamy and absent; possibly she was tired </s>
<s> Her life was in imminent danger, and she did not suspect it </s>
<s> The time was ripe now, and Beaupere quietly and stealthily sprang his trap: "Are you in a state of Grace" </s>

<s> The accused is not obliged to answer it" </s>

<s> and take your seat </s>
<s> The accused will answer the question" </s>
<s> There was no hope, no way out of the dilemma; for whether she said yes or whether she said no, it would be all the same--a disastrous answer, for the Scriptures had said one cannot know this thing </s>

<s> He asked Joan a thousand questions about her childhood and about the oak wood, and the fairies, and the children's games and romps under our dear Arbre Fee Bourlemont, and this stirring up of old memories broke her voice and made her cry a little, but she bore up as well as she could, and answered everything </s>
<s> Then the priest finished by touching again upon the matter of her apparel--a matter which was never to be lost sight of in this still-hunt for this innocent creature's life, but kept always hanging over her, a menace charged with mournful possibilities: "Would you like a woman's dress" </s>
<s> "Indeed yes, if I may go out from this prison--but here, no" </s>
<s> 8 Joan Tells of Her Visions THE COURT met next on Monday the 27th </s>
<s> Would you believe it </s>
<s> The Bishop ignored the contract limiting the examination to matters set down in the proces verbal and again commanded Joan to take the oath without reservations </s>

<s> She stood her ground, and Cauchon had to yield </s>
<s> The examination was resumed, concerning Joan's Voices </s>

<s> Thus closed a weary long sitting, without result </s>
<s> Every device that could be contrived to trap Joan into wrong thinking, wrong doing, or disloyalty to the Church, or sinfulness as a little child at home or later, had been tried, and none of them had succeeded </s>
<s> She had come unscathed through the ordeal </s>
<s> Was the court discouraged </s>
<s> No </s>
<s> Naturally it was very much surprised, very much astonished, to find its work baffling and difficult instead of simple and easy, but it had powerful allies in the shape of hunger, cold, fatigue, persecution, deception, and treachery; and opposed to this array nothing but a defenseless and ignorant girl who must some time or other surrender to bodily and mental exhaustion or get caught in one of the thousand traps set for her </s>
<s> And had the court made no progress during these seemingly resultless sittings </s>
<s> Yes </s>
<s> It had been feeling its way, groping here, groping there, and had found one or two vague trails which might freshen by and by and lead to something </s>
<s> The male attire, for instance, and the visions and Voices </s>
<s> Of course no one doubted that she had seen supernatural beings and been spoken to and advised by them </s>
<s> And of course no one doubted that by supernatural help miracles had been done by Joan, such as choosing out the King in a crowd when she had never seen him before, and her discovery of the sword buried under the altar </s>
<s> It would have been foolish to doubt these things, for we all know that the air is full of devils and angels that are visible to traffickers in magic on the one hand and to the stainlessly holy on the other; but what many and perhaps most did doubt was, that Joan's visions, Voices, and miracles came from God </s>
<s> It was hoped that in time they could be proven to have been of satanic origin </s>
<s> Therefore, as you see, the court's persistent fashion of coming back to that subject every little while and spooking around it and prying into it was not to pass the time--it had a strictly business end in view </s>
<s> 9 Her Sure Deliverance Foretold THE NEXT sitting opened on Thursday the first of March </s>
<s> Fifty-eight judges present--the others resting </s>
<s> As usual, Joan was required to take an oath without reservations </s>
<s> She showed no temper this time </s>
<s> She considered herself well buttressed by the proces verbal compromise which Cauchon was so anxious to repudiate and creep out of; so she merely refused, distinctly and decidedly; and added, in a spirit of fairness and candor: "But as to matters set down in the proces verbal, I will freely tell the whole truth--yes, as freely and fully as if I were before the Pope" </s>
<s> Here was a chance </s>
<s> We had two or three Popes, then; only one of them could be the true Pope, of course </s>
<s> Everybody judiciously shirked the question of which was the true Pope and refrained from naming him, it being clearly dangerous to go into particulars in this matter </s>
<s> Here was an opportunity to trick an unadvised girl into bringing herself into peril, and the unfair judge lost no time in taking advantage of it </s>
<s> He asked, in a plausibly indolent and absent way: "Which one do you consider to be the true Pope" </s>
<s> The house took an attitude of deep attention, and so waited to hear the answer and see the prey walk into the trap </s>
<s> But when the answer came it covered the judge with confusion, and you could see many people covertly chuckling </s>
<s> For Joan asked in a voice and manner which almost deceived even me, so innocent it seemed: "Are there two" </s>
<s> One of the ablest priests in that body and one of the best swearers there, spoke right out so that half the house heard him, and said: "By God, it was a master stroke" </s>
<s> As soon as the judge was better of his embarrassment he came back to the charge, but was prudent and passed by Joan's question: "Is it true that you received a letter from the Count of Armagnac asking you which of the three Popes he ought to obey" </s>
<s> "Yes, and answered it" </s>
<s> Copies of both letters were produced and read </s>
<s> Joan said that hers had not been quite strictly copied </s>
<s> She said she had received the Count's letter when she was just mounting her horse; and added: "So, in dictating a word or two of reply I said I would try to answer him from Paris or somewhere where I could be at rest" </s>
<s> She was asked again which Pope she had considered the right one </s>
<s> "I was not able to instruct the Count of Armagnac as to which one he ought to obey"; then she added, with a frank fearlessness which sounded fresh and wholesome in that den of trimmers and shufflers, "but as for me, I hold that we are bound to obey our Lord the Pope who is at Rome" </s>
<s> The matter was dropped </s>
<s> They produced and read a copy of Joan's first effort at dictating--her proclamation summoning the English to retire from the siege of Orleans and vacate France--truly a great and fine production for an unpractised girl of seventeen </s>
<s> "Do you acknowledge as your own the document which has just been read" </s>
<s> "Yes, except that there are errors in it--words which make me give myself too much importance" </s>
<s> I saw what was coming; I was troubled and ashamed </s>
<s> "For instance, I did not say 'Deliver up to the Maid' (rendez au la Pucelle); I said 'Deliver up to the King' (rendez au Roi); and I did not call myself 'Commander-in-Chief' (chef de guerre) </s>
<s> All those are words which my secretary substituted; or mayhap he misheard me or forgot what I said" </s>
<s> She did not look at me when she said it: she spared me that embarrassment </s>
<s> I hadn't misheard her at all, and hadn't forgotten </s>
<s> I changed her language purposely, for she was Commander-in-Chief and entitled to call herself so, and it was becoming and proper, too; and who was going to surrender anything to the King?--at that time a stick, a cipher </s>
<s> If any surrendering was done, it would be to the noble Maid of Vaucouleurs, already famed and formidable though she had not yet struck a blow </s>
<s> Ah, there would have been a fine and disagreeable episode (for me) there, if that pitiless court had discovered that the very scribbler of that piece of dictation, secretary to Joan of Arc, was present--and not only present, but helping build the record; and not only that, but destined at a far distant day to testify against lies and perversions smuggled into it by Cauchon and deliver them over to eternal infamy </s>
<s> "Do you acknowledge that you dictated this proclamation" </s>
<s> "I do" </s>
<s> "Have you repented of it </s>
<s> Do you retract it" </s>
<s> Ah, then she was indignant </s>
<s> "No </s>
<s> Not even these chains"--and she shook them--"not even these chains can chill the hopes that I uttered there </s>
<s> And more"!--she rose, and stood a moment with a divine strange light kindling in her face, then her words burst forth as in a flood--"I warn you now that before seven years a disaster will smite the English, oh, many fold greater than the fall of Orleans </s>
<s> and--" "Silence </s>
<s> Sit down" </s>
<s> "--and then, soon after, they will lose all France" </s>
<s> Now consider these things </s>
<s> The French armies no longer existed </s>
<s> The French cause was standing still, our King was standing still, there was no hint that by and by the Constable Richemont would come forward and take up the great work of Joan of Arc and finish it </s>
<s> In face of all this, Joan made that prophecy--made it with perfect confidence--and it came true </s>
<s> For within five years Paris fell--1436--and our King marched into it flying the victor's flag </s>
<s> So the first part of the prophecy was then fulfilled--in fact, almost the entire prophecy; for, with Paris in our hands, the fulfilment of the rest of it was assured </s>
<s> Twenty years later all France was ours excepting a single town--Calais </s>
<s> Now that will remind you of an earlier prophecy of Joan's </s>
<s> At the time that she wanted to take Paris and could have done it with ease if our King had but consented, she said that that was the golden time; that, with Paris ours, all France would be ours in six months </s>
<s> But if this golden opportunity to recover France was wasted, said she, "I give you twenty years to do it in" </s>
<s> She was right </s>
<s> After Paris fell, in 1436, the rest of the work had to be done city by city, castle by castle, and it took twenty years to finish it </s>
<s> Yes, it was the first day of March, 1431, there in the court, that she stood in the view of everybody and uttered that strange and incredible prediction </s>
<s> Now and then, in this world, somebody's prophecy turns up correct, but when you come to look into it there is sure to be considerable room for suspicion that the prophecy was made after the fact </s>
<s> But here the matter is different </s>
<s> There in that court Joan's prophecy was set down in the official record at the hour and moment of its utterance, years before the fulfilment, and there you may read it to this day </s>
<s> Twenty-five years after Joan's death the record was produced in the great Court of the Rehabilitation and verified under oath by Manchon and me, and surviving judges of our court confirmed the exactness of the record in their testimony </s>
<s> Joan' startling utterance on that now so celebrated first of March stirred up a great turmoil, and it was some time before it quieted down again </s>
<s> Naturally, everybody was troubled, for a prophecy is a grisly and awful thing, whether one thinks it ascends from hell or comes down from heaven </s>
<s> All that these people felt sure of was, that the inspiration back of it was genuine and puissant </s>
<s> They would have given their right hands to know the source of it </s>
<s> At last the questions began again </s>
<s> "How do you know that those things are going to happen" </s>
<s> "I know it by revelation </s>
<s> And I know it as surely as I know that you sit here before me" </s>
<s> This sort of answer was not going to allay the spreading uneasiness </s>
<s> Therefore, after some further dallying the judge got the subject out of the way and took up one which he could enjoy more </s>
<s> "What languages do your Voices speak" </s>
<s> "French" </s>
<s> "St </s>
<s> Marguerite, too" </s>
<s> "Verily; why not </s>
<s> She is on our side, not on the English" </s>
<s> Saints and angels who did not condescend to speak English is a grave affront </s>
<s> They could not be brought into court and punished for contempt, but the tribunal could take silent note of Joan's remark and remember it against her; which they did </s>
<s> It might be useful by and by </s>
<s> "Do your saints and angels wear jewelry?--crowns, rings, earrings" </s>
<s> To Joan, questions like these were profane frivolities and not worthy of serious notice; she answered indifferently </s>
<s> But the question brought to her mind another matter, and she turned upon Cauchon and said: "I had two rings </s>
<s> They have been taken away from me during my captivity </s>
<s> You have one of them </s>
<s> It is the gift of my brother </s>
<s> Give it back to me </s>
<s> If not to me, then I pray that it be given to the Church" </s>
<s> The judges conceived the idea that maybe these rings were for the working of enchantments </s>
<s> Perhaps they could be made to do Joan a damage </s>
<s> "Where is the other ring" </s>
<s> "The Burgundians have it" </s>
<s> "Where did you get it" </s>
<s> "My father and mother gave it to me" </s>
<s> "Describe it" </s>
<s> "It is plain and simple and has 'Jesus and Mary' engraved upon it" </s>
<s> Everybody could see that that was not a valuable equipment to do devil's work with </s>
<s> So that trail was not worth following </s>
<s> Still, to make sure, one of the judges asked Joan if she had ever cured sick people by touching them with the ring </s>
<s> She said no </s>
<s> "Now as concerning the fairies, that were used to abide near by Domremy whereof there are many reports and traditions </s>
<s> It is said that your godmother surprised these creatures on a summer's night dancing under the tree called l'Arbre Fee de Bourlemont </s>
<s> Is it not possible that your pretended saints and angels are but those fairies" </s>
<s> "Is that in your proces" </s>
<s> She made no other answer </s>
<s> "Have you not conversed with St </s>
<s> Marguerite and St </s>
<s> Catherine under that tree" </s>
<s> "I do not know" </s>
<s> "Or by the fountain near the tree" </s>
<s> "Yes, sometimes" </s>
<s> "What promises did they make you" </s>
<s> "None but such as they had God's warrant for" </s>
<s> "But what promises did they make" </s>
<s> "That is not in your proces; yet I will say this much: they told me that the King would become master of his kingdom in spite of his enemies" </s>
<s> "And what else" </s>
<s> There was a pause; then she said humbly: "They promised to lead me to Paradise" </s>
<s> If faces do really betray what is passing in men's minds, a fear came upon many in that house, at this time, that maybe, after all, a chosen servant and herald of God was here being hunted to her death </s>
<s> The interest deepened </s>
<s> Movements and whisperings ceased: the stillness became almost painful </s>
<s> Have you noticed that almost from the beginning the nature of the questions asked Joan showed that in some way or other the questioner very often already knew his fact before he asked his question </s>
<s> Have you noticed that somehow or other the questioners usually knew just how and were to search for Joan's secrets; that they really knew the bulk of her privacies--a fact not suspected by her--and that they had no task before them but to trick her into exposing those secrets </s>
<s> Do you remember Loyseleur, the hypocrite, the treacherous priest, tool of Cauchon </s>
<s> Do you remember that under the sacred seal of the confessional Joan freely and trustingly revealed to him everything concerning her history save only a few things regarding her supernatural revelations which her Voices had forbidden her to tell to any one--and that the unjust judge, Cauchon, was a hidden listener all the time </s>
<s> Now you understand how the inquisitors were able to devise that long array of minutely prying questions; questions whose subtlety and ingenuity and penetration are astonishing until we come to remember Loyseleur's performance and recognize their source </s>
<s> Ah, Bishop of Beauvais, you are now lamenting this cruel iniquity these many years in hell </s>
<s> Yes verily, unless one has come to your help </s>
<s> There is but one among the redeemed that would do it; and it is futile to hope that that one has not already done it--Joan of Arc </s>
<s> We will return to the questionings </s>
<s> "Did they make you still another promise" </s>
<s> "Yes, but that is not in your proces </s>
<s> I will not tell it now, but before three months I will tell it you" </s>
<s> The judge seems to know the matter he is asking about, already; one gets this idea from his next question </s>
<s> "Did your Voices tell you that you would be liberated before three months" </s>
<s> Joan often showed a little flash of surprise at the good guessing of the judges, and she showed one this time </s>
<s> I was frequently in terror to find my mind (which I could not control) criticizing the Voices and saying, "They counsel her to speak boldly--a thing which she would do without any suggestion from them or anybody else--but when it comes to telling her any useful thing, such as how these conspirators manage to guess their way so skilfully into her affairs, they are always off attending to some other business" </s>
<s> I am reverent by nature; and when such thoughts swept through my head they made me cold with fear, and if there was a storm and thunder at the time, I was so ill that I could but with difficulty abide at my post and do my work </s>
<s> Joan answered: "That is not in your proces </s>
<s> I do not know when I shall be set free, but some who wish me out of this world will go from it before me" </s>
<s> It made some of them shiver </s>
<s> "Have your Voices told you that you will be delivered from this prison" </s>
<s> Without a doubt they had, and the judge knew it before he asked the question </s>
<s> "Ask me again in three months and I will tell you" </s>
<s> She said it with such a happy look, the tired prisoner </s>
<s> And I </s>
<s> And Noel Rainguesson, drooping yonder?--why, the floods of joy went streaming through us from crown to sole </s>
<s> It was all that we could do to hold still and keep from making fatal exposure of our feelings </s>
<s> She was to be set free in three months </s>
<s> That was what she meant; we saw it </s>
<s> The Voices had told her so, and told her true--true to the very day--May 30th </s>
<s> But we know now that they had mercifully hidden from her how she was to be set free, but left her in ignorance </s>
<s> Home again </s>
<s> That day was our understanding of it--Noel's and mine; that was our dream; and now we would count the days, the hours, the minutes </s>
<s> They would fly lightly along; they would soon be over </s>
<s> Yes, we would carry our idol home; and there, far from the pomps and tumults of the world, we would take up our happy life again and live it out as we had begun it, in the free air and the sunshine, with the friendly sheep and the friendly people for comrades, and the grace and charm of the meadows, the woods, and the river always before our eyes and their deep peace in our hearts </s>
<s> Yes, that was our dream, the dream that carried us bravely through that three months to an exact and awful fulfilment, the thought of which would have killed us, I think, if we had foreknown it and been obliged to bear the burden of it upon our hearts the half of those weary days </s>
<s> Our reading of the prophecy was this: We believed the King's soul was going to be smitten with remorse; and that he would privately plan a rescue with Joan's old lieutenants, D'Alencon and the Bastard and La Hire, and that this rescue would take place at the end of the three months </s>
<s> So we made up our minds to be ready and take a hand in it </s>
<s> In the present and also in later sittings Joan was urged to name the exact day of her deliverance; but she could not do that </s>
<s> She had not the permission of her Voices </s>
<s> Moreover, the Voices themselves did not name the precise day </s>
<s> Ever since the fulfilment of the prophecy, I have believed that Joan had the idea that her deliverance was going to come in the form of death </s>
<s> But not that death </s>
<s> Divine as she was, dauntless as she was in battle, she was human also </s>
<s> She was not solely a saint, an angel, she was a clay-made girl also--as human a girl as any in the world, and full of a human girl's sensitiveness and tenderness and delicacies </s>
<s> And so, that death </s>
<s> No, she could not have lived the three months with that one before her, I think </s>
<s> You remember that the first time she was wounded she was frightened, and cried, just as any other girl of seventeen would have done, although she had known for eighteen days that she was going to be wounded on that very day </s>
<s> No, she was not afraid of any ordinary death, and an ordinary death was what she believed the prophecy of deliverance meant, I think, for her face showed happiness, not horror, when she uttered it </s>
<s> Now I will explain why I think as I do </s>
<s> Five weeks before she was captured in the battle of Compiegne, her Voices told her what was coming </s>
<s> They did not tell her the day or the place, but said she would be taken prisoner and that it would be before the feast of St </s>
<s> John </s>
<s> She begged that death, certain and swift, should be her fate, and the captivity brief; for she was a free spirit, and dreaded the confinement </s>
<s> The Voices made no promise, but only told her to bear whatever came </s>
<s> Now as they did not refuse the swift death, a hopeful young thing like Joan would naturally cherish that fact and make the most of it, allowing it to grow and establish itself in her mind </s>
<s> And so now that she was told she was to be "delivered" in three months, I think she believed it meant that she would die in her bed in the prison, and that that was why she looked happy and content--the gates of Paradise standing open for her, the time so short, you see, her troubles so soon to be over, her reward so close at hand </s>
<s> Yes, that would make her look happy, that would make her patient and bold, and able to fight her fight out like a soldier </s>
<s> Save herself if she could, of course, and try for the best, for that was the way she was made; but die with her face to the front if die she must </s>
<s> Then later, when she charged Cauchon with trying to kill her with a poisoned fish, her notion that she was to be "delivered" by death in the prison--if she had it, and I believe she had--would naturally be greatly strengthened, you see </s>
<s> But I am wandering from the trial </s>
<s> Joan was asked to definitely name the time that she would be delivered from prison </s>
<s> "I have always said that I was not permitted to tell you everything </s>
<s> I am to be set free, and I desire to ask leave of my Voices to tell you the day </s>
<s> That is why I wish for delay" </s>
<s> "Do your Voices forbid you to tell the truth" </s>
<s> "Is it that you wish to know matters concerning the King of France </s>
<s> I tell you again that he will regain his kingdom, and that I know it as well as I know that you sit here before me in this tribunal" </s>
<s> She sighed and, after a little pause, added: "I should be dead but for this revelation, which comforts me always" </s>
<s> Some trivial questions were asked her about St </s>
<s> Michael's dress and appearance </s>
<s> She answered them with dignity, but one saw that they gave her pain </s>
<s> After a little she said: "I have great joy in seeing him, for when I see him I have the feeling that I am not in mortal sin" </s>
<s> She added, "Sometimes St </s>
<s> Marguerite and St </s>
<s> Catherine have allowed me to confess myself to them" </s>
<s> Here was a possible chance to set a successful snare for her innocence </s>
<s> "When you confessed were you in mortal sin, do you think" </s>
<s> But her reply did her no hurt </s>
<s> So the inquiry was shifted once more to the revelations made to the King--secrets which the court had tried again and again to force out of Joan, but without success </s>
<s> "Now as to the sign given to the King--" "I have already told you that I will tell you nothing about it" </s>
<s> "Do you know what the sign was" </s>
<s> "As to that, you will not find out from me" </s>
<s> All this refers to Joan's secret interview with the King--held apart, though two or three others were present </s>
<s> It was known--through Loyseleur, of course--that this sign was a crown and was a pledge of the verity of Joan's mission </s>
<s> But that is all a mystery until this day--the nature of the crown, I mean--and will remain a mystery to the end of time </s>
<s> We can never know whether a real crown descended upon the King's head, or only a symbol, the mystic fabric of a vision </s>
<s> "Did you see a crown upon the King's head when he received the revelation" </s>
<s> "I cannot tell you as to that, without perjury" </s>
<s> "Did the King have that crown at Rheims" </s>
<s> "I think the King put upon his head a crown which he found there; but a much richer one was brought him afterward" </s>
<s> "Have you seen that one" </s>
<s> "I cannot tell you, without perjury </s>
<s> But whether I have seen it or not, I have heard say that it was rich and magnificent" </s>
<s> They went on and pestered her to weariness about that mysterious crown, but they got nothing more out of her </s>
<s> The sitting closed </s>
<s> A long, hard day for all of us </s>
<s> 10 The Inquisitors at Their Wits' End THE COURT rested a day, then took up work again on Saturday, the third of March </s>
<s> This was one of our stormiest sessions </s>
<s> The whole court was out of patience; and with good reason </s>
<s> These threescore distinguished churchmen, illustrious tacticians, veteran legal gladiators, had left important posts where their supervision was needed, to journey hither from various regions and accomplish a most simple and easy matter--condemn and send to death a country-lass of nineteen who could neither read nor write, knew nothing of the wiles and perplexities of legal procedure, could not call a single witness in her defense, was allowed no advocate or adviser, and must conduct her case by herself against a hostile judge and a packed jury </s>
<s> In two hours she would be hopelessly entangled, routed, defeated, convicted </s>
<s> Nothing could be more certain that this--so they thought </s>
<s> But it was a mistake </s>
<s> The two hours had strung out into days; what promised to be a skirmish had expanded into a siege; the thing which had looked so easy had proven to be surprisingly difficult; the light victim who was to have been puffed away like a feather remained planted like a rock; and on top of all this, if anybody had a right to laugh it was the country-lass and not the court </s>
<s> She was not doing that, for that was not her spirit; but others were doing it </s>
<s> The whole town was laughing in its sleeve, and the court knew it, and its dignity was deeply hurt </s>
<s> The members could not hide their annoyance </s>
<s> And so, as I have said, the session was stormy </s>
<s> It was easy to see that these men had made up their minds to force words from Joan to-day which should shorten up her case and bring it to a prompt conclusion </s>
<s> It shows that after all their experience with her they did not know her yet </s>
<s> They went into the battle with energy </s>
<s> They did not leave the questioning to a particular member; no, everybody helped </s>
<s> They volleyed questions at Joan from all over the house, and sometimes so many were talking at once that she had to ask them to deliver their fire one at a time and not by platoons </s>
<s> The beginning was as usual: "You are once more required to take the oath pure and simple" </s>
<s> "I will answer to what is in the proces verbal </s>
<s> When I do more, I will choose the occasion for myself" </s>
<s> That old ground was debated and fought over inch by inch with great bitterness and many threats </s>
<s> But Joan remained steadfast, and the questionings had to shift to other matters </s>
<s> Half an hour was spent over Joan's apparitions--their dress, hair, general appearance, and so on--in the hope of fishing something of a damaging sort out of the replies; but with no result </s>
<s> Next, the male attire was reverted to, of course </s>
<s> After many well-worn questions had been re-asked, one or two new ones were put forward </s>
<s> "Did not the King or the Queen sometimes ask you to quit the male dress" </s>
<s> "That is not in your proces" </s>
<s> "Do you think you would have sinned if you had taken the dress of your sex" </s>
<s> "I have done best to serve and obey my sovereign Lord and Master" </s>
<s> After a while the matter of Joan's Standard was taken up, in the hope of connecting magic and witchcraft with it </s>
<s> "Did not your men copy your banner in their pennons" </s>
<s> "The lancers of my guard did it </s>
<s> It was to distinguish them from the rest of the forces </s>
<s> It was their own idea" </s>
<s> "Were they often renewed" </s>
<s> "Yes </s>
<s> When the lances were broken they were renewed" </s>
<s> The purpose of the question unveils itself in the next one </s>
<s> "Did you not say to your men that pennons made like your banner would be lucky" </s>
<s> The soldier-spirit in Joan was offended at this puerility </s>
<s> She drew herself up, and said with dignity and fire: "What I said to them was, 'Ride those English down' </s>
<s> and I did it myself" </s>
<s> Whenever she flung out a scornful speech like that at these French menials in English livery it lashed them into a rage; and that is what happened this time </s>
<s> There were ten, twenty, sometimes even thirty of them on their feet at a time, storming at the prisoner minute after minute, but Joan was not disturbed </s>
<s> By and by there was peace, and the inquiry was resumed </s>
<s> It was now sought to turn against Joan the thousand loving honors which had been done her when she was raising France out of the dirt and shame of a century of slavery and castigation </s>
<s> "Did you not cause paintings and images of yourself to be made" </s>
<s> "No </s>
<s> At Arras I saw a painting of myself kneeling in armor before the King and delivering him a letter; but I caused no such things to be made" </s>
<s> "Were not masses and prayers said in your honor" </s>
<s> "If it was done it was not by my command </s>
<s> But if any prayed for me I think it was no harm" </s>
<s> "Did the French people believe you were sent of God" </s>
<s> "As to that, I know not; but whether they believed it or not, I was not the less sent of God" </s>
<s> "If they thought you were sent of God, do you think it was well thought" </s>
<s> "If they believed it, their trust was not abused" </s>
<s> "What impulse was it, think you, that moved the people to kiss your hands, your feet, and your vestments" </s>
<s> "They were glad to see me, and so they did those things; and I could not have prevented them if I had had the heart </s>
<s> Those poor people came lovingly to me because I had not done them any hurt, but had done the best I could for them according to my strength" </s>
<s> See what modest little words she uses to describe that touching spectacle, her marches about France walled in on both sides by the adoring multitudes: "They were glad to see me" </s>
<s> Glad </s>
<s> Why they were transported with joy to see her </s>
<s> When they could not kiss her hands or her feet, they knelt in the mire and kissed the hoof-prints of her horse </s>
<s> They worshiped her; and that is what these priests were trying to prove </s>
<s> It was nothing to them that she was not to blame for what other people did </s>
<s> No, if she was worshiped, it was enough; she was guilty of mortal sin </s>
<s> Curious logic, one must say </s>
<s> "Did you not stand sponsor for some children baptized at Rheims" </s>
<s> "At Troyes I did, and at St </s>
<s> Denis; and I named the boys Charles, in honor of the King, and the girls I named Joan" </s>
<s> "Did not women touch their rings to those which you wore" </s>
<s> "Yes, many did, but I did not know their reason for it" </s>
<s> "At Rheims was your Standard carried into the church </s>
<s> Did you stand at the altar with it in your hand at the Coronation" </s>
<s> "Yes" </s>
<s> "In passing through the country did you confess yourself in the Churches and receive the sacrament" </s>
<s> "Yes" </s>
<s> "In the dress of a man" </s>
<s> "Yes </s>
<s> But I do not remember that I was in armor" </s>
<s> It was almost a concession </s>
<s> almost a half-surrender of the permission granted her by the Church at Poitiers to dress as a man </s>
<s> The wily court shifted to another matter: to pursue this one at this time might call Joan's attention to her small mistake, and by her native cleverness she might recover her lost ground </s>
<s> The tempestuous session had worn her and drowsed her alertness </s>
<s> "It is reported that you brought a dead child to life in the church at Lagny </s>
<s> Was that in answer to your prayers" </s>
<s> "As to that, I have no knowledge </s>
<s> Other young girls were praying for the child, and I joined them and prayed also, doing no more than they" </s>
<s> "Continue" </s>
<s> "While we prayed it came to life, and cried </s>
<s> It had been dead three days, and was as black as my doublet </s>
<s> It was straight way baptized, then it passed from life again and was buried in holy ground" </s>
<s> "Why did you jump from the tower of Beaurevoir by night and try to escape" </s>
<s> "I would go to the succor of Compiegne" </s>
<s> It was insinuated that this was an attempt to commit the deep crime of suicide to avoid falling into the hands of the English </s>

<s> 11 The Court Reorganized for Assassination A HALT was called </s>
<s> It was time </s>

<s> (1) What she said has been many times translated, but never with success </s>

<s> 12 Joan's Master-Stroke Diverted NOW, as a next move, this small secret court of holy assassins did a thing so base that even at this day, in my old age, it is hard to speak of it with patience </s>
<s> In the beginning of her commerce with her Voices there at Domremy, the child Joan solemnly devoted her life to God, vowing her pure body and her pure soul to His service </s>
<s> You will remember that her parents tried to stop her from going to the wars by haling her to the court at Toul to compel her to make a marriage which she had never promised to make--a marriage with our poor, good, windy, big, hard-fighting, and most dear and lamented comrade, the Standard-Bearer, who fell in honorable battle and sleeps with God these sixty years, peace to his ashes </s>
<s> And you will remember how Joan, sixteen years old, stood up in that venerable court and conducted her case all by herself, and tore the poor Paladin's case to rags and blew it away with a breath; and how the astonished old judge on the bench spoke of her as "this marvelous child" </s>
<s> You remember all that </s>
<s> Then think what I felt, to see these false priests, here in the tribunal wherein Joan had fought a fourth lone fight in three years, deliberately twist that matter entirely around and try to make out that Joan haled the Paladin into court and pretended that he had promised to marry her, and was bent on making him do it </s>
<s> Certainly there was no baseness that those people were ashamed to stoop to in their hunt for that friendless girl's life </s>
<s> What they wanted to show was this--that she had committed the sin of relapsing from her vow and trying to violate it </s>
<s> Joan detailed the true history of the case, but lost her temper as she went along, and finished with some words for Cauchon which he remembers yet, whether he is fanning himself in the world he belongs in or has swindled his way into the other </s>

<s> It was shabby work for those grave men to be engaged in; for they well knew one of Joan's reasons for clinging to the male dress was, that soldiers of the guard were always present in her room whether she was asleep or awake, and that the male dress was a better protection for her modesty than the other </s>
<s> The court knew that one of Joan's purposes had been the deliverance of the exiled Duke of Orleans, and they were curious to know how she had intended to manage it </s>

<s> If a thing was to be done, it was love first, and hammer and tongs to follow; but no shilly-shallying between </s>

<s> We were now arriving at the last day of this new trial </s>
<s> Joan had come through the ordeal well </s>
<s> It had been a long and wearisome struggle for all concerned </s>
<s> All ways had been tried to convict the accused, and all had failed, thus far </s>

<s> The court took note of this straitly worded refusal, and would hope to get profit out of it; but the matter was dropped for the present, and a long chase was then made over the old hunting-ground--the fairies, the visions, the male attire, and all that </s>
<s> In the afternoon the satanic Bishop himself took the chair and presided over the closing scenes of the trial </s>

<s> Would you not answer the Pope more fully than you have answered before my lord of Beauvais </s>
<s> Would you not feel obliged to answer the Pope, who is the Vicar of God, more fully" </s>

<s> It made the Bishop's purple face fairly blanch with consternation </s>
<s> If Joan had only known, if she had only know </s>
<s> She had lodged a mine under this black conspiracy able to blow the Bishop's schemes to the four winds of heaven, and she didn't know it </s>
